 monosodium glutamet (MSG) swaad badhaane ke liye khaane kii chizon main daalaa jaataa he

 MSG kam maatra main lene se surakshit hota he lekin jin logon ko isse allergy ho, unke liye kam maatra main bhi iskaa seven khatarnaak ho saktaa he
 The thing to note is that processed foods like chips, packaged soups, canned food, MSG is present in more quantity
 processd food pehle se hi nuksaandaayak hote hai or MSG kii vajah se or bhi nuksaan pahunchaata he
 Before buying anything, check whether the MSG is present on the packet
 agar ingradient main MSG likhaa ho to us cheez ko khaane se bachein
 Chemically there is no difference between the naturally occurring MSG and MSG present in processed foods
 lekin processd food main zyada maatra main MSG hone yaa duusare nuksaandaayak tatwon kii maujuudagi kii vajah se zyada khatarnaak sabit ho saktaa he
 It occurs in such things as canned food, sauces, chips, packet soup, hot dogs, beer
 iske alaava paneer, tamaato, matar, walnuts, gehun main prakritik taur par maujuud hota he
 High doses of sodium glutamate are associated with increased appetite, obesity, and other metabolic disorders
 sodium glutamet ke zyada seven se migraine, susti, hormone asantulan, ultiyaan, kamajori, seene main dard jaisi samasyaayein ho sakati hai
 This increases the taste of food due to which people eat more
 nateeja motopa or zyada vajan ke rup main saamne aata he
 Sodium glutamate has a drug-like effect on brain cells
 kai studies main bataaya gaya he ki khaane main sodium glutamet kii maatra badhane se diabetes ke bhi maamle bade hai
 Excess intake of this affects the action of the adrenal gland, high blood pressure, hypertension, and stroke also present dangers

 2- shaam mata parvati or shivaji ke pujan kii taiyaari karen
